  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/417648757" />
    <a title="Marissa (Rae Gun Ramblings)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4654387-marissa-rae-gun-ramblings"><img alt="Marissa (Rae Gun Ramblings)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1292221709p2/4654387.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/417648757?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marissa (Rae Gun Ramblings)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marissa (Rae Gun Ramblings)" href="/user/show/4654387-marissa-rae-gun-ramblings">Marissa (Rae Gun Ramblings)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4654387-marissa-rae-gun-ramblings?shelf=so-excited-sequels">so-excited-sequels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4654387-marissa-rae-gun-ramblings?shelf=review-wish-list">review-wish-list</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer417648757" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11494548791044556398">Fragments picks right up where Partials left off. You jump straight into the action. Kira, Marcus and the rest of the crew that I grew to love are back but they find themselves separated. There is little communication between the groups yet they are all working toward the same goal and it it so fun to see how the work Marcus's team compliments what Kira is up to. While like the first one the romance is kept to a minimum, there is one of my favorite couple-y lines of dialogue in this book. Like w</span>
  <span id="freeText11494548791044556398" style="display:none">Fragments picks right up where Partials left off. You jump straight into the action. Kira, Marcus and the rest of the crew that I grew to love are back but they find themselves separated. There is little communication between the groups yet they are all working toward the same goal and it it so fun to see how the work Marcus's team compliments what Kira is up to. While like the first one the romance is kept to a minimum, there is one of my favorite couple-y lines of dialogue in this book. Like with the first book it took me a little time to be sucked in but once that happened I was hooked. <br /><br />The story unfolds giving us even more of Samm who is mostly a mystery to us at the end of the first book but if you are anything like me you wanted to know more. Don't worry we get A LOT of Samm. And surprisingly Heron plays a bigger role. I would have never guessed but I ended up loving Heron. Not that I was ever quite sure what side she was on, her sass and cold but comical ways had me laughing throughout the book. <br /><br />I'm not going to lie this one was a little stressful. Between juggling the crazy political climate, learning how deep and complicated the history of RM and the Partials went I found myself reading until early in the morning and wired from all the craziness. And yes we get even more of the awesome science fiction but surprising to me I even found myself tear up. There are many surprises as the next installment of this story unfolds. I definitely recommend it. <br /><br />I received an advance copy for review but this review is 100% my honest opinion</span>
  <a data-text-id="11494548791044556398" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_10193062'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10193062-outpost"><img alt="Outpost (Razorland, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1343084394l/10193062._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hK5EoY2CU628S7pOzy7Jd8TrVajNGwALxrWGABPFgEgjeZHhKYo9mvCxhoYa7oPtnGLeCalPK3IGlb6Jog9paQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10489284052942651508">Dan Wells is a thriller and science fiction writer. Born in Utah, he spent his early years reading and writing. He is he author of the Partials series (Partials, Isolation, Fragments, and Ruins), the John Cleaver series (I Am Not a Serial Killer, Mr. Monster, and I Don't Want To Kill You), and a few others (The Hollow City, A Night of Blacker Darkness, etc). He was a Campbell nomine for best new w</span>
  <span id="freeText10489284052942651508" style="display:none">Dan Wells is a thriller and science fiction writer. Born in Utah, he spent his early years reading and writing. He is he author of the Partials series (Partials, Isolation, Fragments, and Ruins), the John Cleaver series (I Am Not a Serial Killer, Mr. Monster, and I Don't Want To Kill You), and a few others (The Hollow City, A Night of Blacker Darkness, etc). He was a Campbell nomine for best new writer, and has won a Hugo award for his work on the podcast Writing Excuses; the podcast is also a multiple winner of the Parsec Award.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10489284052942651508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
